<p dir="auto"><strong>Inria</strong> and <strong>the Max Planck Institut for Informatik (MPII)</strong> hold all the ownership rights on the <em>Software</em> named <strong>gaussian-splatting</strong>.<br>
The <em>Software</em> is in the process of being registered with the Agence pour la Protection des<br>
Programmes (APP).</p>
<p dir="auto">The <em>Software</em> is still being developed by the <em>Licensor</em>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><em>Licensor</em>'s goal is to allow the research community to use, test and evaluate<br>
the <em>Software</em>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1.  Definitions</h2><a id="user-content-1--definitions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1.
